\section{CloudUsageBlock}


  		





  2
  4
  
    

  		





  3
  5
  
    
This block contains the properties related to cloud usage.


  		





  ......




  51
  53
  
    
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


  		





  52
  54
  
    

  		





  53
  55
  
    

  		





  54
  
  
    
\subsection{SuspendTime}


  		





  
  56
  
    
\subsection{SuspendDuration}


  		





  55
  57
  
    

  		





  56
  
  
    
\emph{SuspendTime} is a value that count for the amount of time in which the Virtual Machine changed status to ``suspended''.


  		





  
  58
  
    
\emph{SuspendDuration} is a value that count for the amount of time in which the Virtual Machine changed status to ``suspended''.


  		





  57
  59
  
    

  		





  58
  60
  
    
\begin{itemize}


  		





  59
  
  
    
\item \emph{SuspendTime} MUST be present when \emph{Status} if the Virtual Machine was suspended ``suspended''.


  		





  60
  
  
    
\item \emph{SuspendTime} field type MUST be an ISO 8601:2004 timestamp.


  		





  
  61
  
    
\item \emph{SuspendDuration} MUST be present when \emph{Status} if the Virtual Machine was suspended ``suspended''.


  		





  
  62
  
    
\item \emph{SuspendDuration} MUST contain a time duration as defined in ISO 8601:2004.


  		





  61
  63
  
    
%\item time zone may be specified as Z (UTC) or (+|-)hh:mm. Time zones that are not specified are considered undetermined.


  		





  62
  64
  
    
\end{itemize}


  		





  63
  65

  32
  32
  
    

  		





  33
  33
  
    
\subsubsection{History}


  		





  34
  34
  
    

  		





  35
  
  
    
Before the definition of UR-2.0, different usage record definitions building on the job accounting definition of UR-1.0\cite{mach2007usagerecord}, started to surface to describe various resource usages, such as the EMI Compute Accounting Reccord (CAR)\cite{guarise2011definition}, the EMI Storage Accounting Record (StAR)\cite{nilsen2011emi} and the EGI Cloud Usage Record (CUR)\footnote{https://wiki.egi.eu/wiki/Fedcloud-tf:WorkGroups:Scenario4}. The definition of UR-2.0 came from the experience of these record definitions and is built as an easily extensible superset of these new usage records.


  		





  
  35
  
    
Before the definition of UR-2.0, different usage record definitions building on the job accounting definition of UR-1.0\cite{mach2007usagerecord}, started to surface to describe various resource usages, such as the EMI Compute Accounting Reccord (CAR)\cite{guarise2011definition}, the EMI Storage Accounting Record (StAR)\cite{nilsen2011emi}, the EGI Cloud Usage Record (CUR)\footnote{https://wiki.egi.eu/wiki/Fedcloud-tf:WorkGroups:Scenario4} and the Storage Accounting Implementation (SAI)\cite{cristofori2011grid}. The definition of UR-2.0 came from the experience of these record definitions and is built as an easily extensible superset of these new usage records.

  36

  38
